NOTIFICATIONS BY GOVERNMENT
HOME  DEPARTMENT
Appointment of Law Oﬃ  cer to the Human Rights Court in 
Cuddalore District on tenure basis under the protection 
of Human Rights Act
[G.O. (D) No. 65, Home (Courts.VIA), 20th January 2022, 
]
No.II(2)/HO/77/2022.—In 
exercise 
of 
the 
powers 
conferred by Section 31 of the protection of Human 
Rights Act, 1993 (Central Act 10 of 1993) the Governor of 
Tamil 
Nadu 
hereby 
appoints 
Thiru. 
V. 
Arulappan, 
S/o, Vaithilingam, No.L-28, Anna Nagar, Cuddalore District 
as Special Public  prosecutor for the purpose of conducting 
cases in Human Rights at the District Court, Cuddalore 
District on tenure basis for a period of three years from 
the date of taking charge of his appointment subject to 
observance of existing  terms and conditions of appointment.
Notiﬁ cations under the Tamil Nadu Protection of Interests 
of Depositors (in Financial  Establishments) Act
Amendments to Notiﬁ cation
Tvl. Rao Investment No.2 C. Glendaden  Place, No.813, 
Poonamallee High Road, Chennai-10.
[G.O. Ms. No. 26, Home (Police XIX), 12th January 2022, 
]
No.II(2)/HO/78/2022.—In 
exercise 
of 
the 
powers 
conferred by Section 3 of the Tamil Nadu protection of 
Interests of Depositors (in Financial Establishments) Act, 
1997 (Tamil Nadu Act 44 of 1997), the Governor of 
Tamil Nadu hereby makes the following amendments to the 
Home Department Notiﬁ cation No.II(2)/HO/69/99, published at 
page 45 of part II-Section 2 of the Tamil Nadu Government 
Gazette, dated the 3rd February, 1999:-
Aඕඍඖඌඕඍඖගඛ
In the said Notiﬁ cation, in the Schedule:
(1) for the expression "Plot No. 25 Measuring 2,430 
Square Feet", the expression "Plot No. 25 Measuring 2,340 
Square Feet", shall be substituted; and
(2) for the expression "(Total Measurement: 11,797 square 
Feet)", the expression "(Total Measurement: 11,707 square 
Feet) " shall be substituted.
Messers Sri Thaimagal Finance Services and 
Sri Thaimagal Corporation, Karur District.
[G.O. Ms. No. 39, Home (Police XIX), 24th January 2022, 
]
No.II(2)/HO/79/2022.—In 
exercise 
of 
the 
powers 
conferred by Section 3 of the Tamil Nadu protection of 
Interests of Depositors (in Financial Establishments) Act, 
1997 (Tamil Nadu Act 44 of 1997), the Governor of 
Tamil Nadu hereby raises the ad-interim order of attachment 
made in Home Department Notiﬁ cation No.II(2)/HO/287/2013, 
published at pages 229 and 230 of part II-Section 2 of the 
Tamil Nadu Government Gazette, dated the 3rd April 2013, 
in respect of properties mentioned against serial Nos. 1,2 
and 3 of the schedule to the said Notiﬁ cation.

Award of the Tamil Nadu Chief Minister’s 
Constabulary Medal on the occasion of 
Pongal Day, 2022
[G.O. Ms. No. 28, Home (SC), 12th January 2022, 
]
No.II(2)/HO/81/2022.—The members of the Tamil Nadu 
Police Force (Men and Women) of the ranks of Police 
Constables Grade-I, Head Constables, Havildars of Armed 
Police and Special Sub-Inspectors of Police, totalling 3000 
whose names are listed in the  Annexure, have been awarded 
the Tamil Nadu Chief Minister’s  Constabulary  Medal   on 
the  occasion of Pongal  Day, 2022   and the recipients are 
eligible to draw a monthly allowance  of Rs.400/- (Rupees 
four hundred only) each.
2. The monthly allowance will be paid with eﬀ ect from 
1st February, 2022.
